<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanmerken.html>aanmerken</a> (77598)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenmerken</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenmercken</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:merken.html>merken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanmerken.html>aanmerken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to comment, to remark <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually suggesting criticism</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opmerken.html>opmerken</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to label, to denote [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a></i> <span>(as)</span></span>] <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to categorise by naming</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:raadsman.html>raadsman</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:merkte.html>merkte</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitspraken.html>uitspraken</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:infame.html>infame</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laster.html>laster</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The attorney <b>qualified</b> the utterances <b>as</b> scandalous libel.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to note, to take notice
<ul><li><b>1784</b>, Elizabeth Wolff amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:agatha.html>Agatha</a> Pieters <a href = vnd.unilang:deken.html>Deken</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:historie.html>Historie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> den <a href = vnd.unilang:heer.html>heer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:willem.html>Willem</a> Leevend</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 1, Isaac <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Cleef (publ.), page 171.
<dl><dd>Gy <a href = vnd.unilang:hebt.html>hebt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bekwaamheid.html>bekwaamheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> onüitspreeklyk <a href = vnd.unilang:lief.html>lief</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> beminlyk <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> zyn; <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zelf.html>zelf</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aanmerken.html>aanmerkt</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> gy <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mooi.html>mooi</a> zyt.</dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:merken.html>merken</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opmerken.html>opmerken</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>assumption</li>

***aanranden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanranden.html>aanranden</a> (38605)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown. Found in late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">anransen</i>. Possibly connected with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rand.html>rand</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> analysed in folk-etymology as if from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">on, to</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rand.html>rand</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">edge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.

***aanrennen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanrennen.html>aanrennen</a> (55218)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">anerennen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to attack</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rennen.html>rennen</a></i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanrennen.html>aanrennen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run near, to run close(<a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>r</a>)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to attack [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(object)</span></span>], to charge [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(against)</span></span>]</li></ol>

***aanrijden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanrijden.html>aanrijden</a> (16160)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenrijden</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rijden.html>rijden</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanrijden.html>aanrijden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to collide with a vehicle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moeder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gister.html>gister</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aangereden.html>aangereden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bus.html>bus</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">My mother <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> hit by the <a href = vnd.unilang:bus.html>bus</a> yesterday.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to arrive driving or riding
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moeder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwam.html>kwam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fiets.html>fiets</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aangereden.html>aangereden</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">My mother <b>arrived</b> by bike.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to depart driving
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moeder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aangereden.html>aangereden</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">My mother just <b>left for</b> home.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Although in common use in the southern Netherlands and Flanders, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:aanrijden.html>aanrijden</a></i> in the sense of <i>to depart</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not generally understood outside of those regions.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanschouw.html>aanschouw</a> (9744)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenschouw</i>, but reinterpreted as a deverbal noun from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanschouwen.html>aanschouwen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanschouw.html>aanschouw</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>sight, appearance <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">that which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> seen</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanblik.html>aanblik</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">aanzicht</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gezicht.html>gezicht</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zicht.html>zicht</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stature, status</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>The feminine gender <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> standard in early modern Dutch, but <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> obsolete since the nineteenth century.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanschouwelijk.html>aanschouwelijk</a> (120160)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanschouwen.html>aanschouwen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanschouwelijk.html>aanschouwelijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanschouwelijk.html>aanschouwelijker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">aanschouwelijkst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>graphical, pictorial</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">visible</span>
<ul><li><b>1838</b>, <i>Noodwendig <a href = vnd.unilang:woordenboek.html>woordenboek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> zamenleving (<a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dames.html>dames</a>). <a href = vnd.unilang:voornamelijk.html>Voornamelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bewerkt.html>bewerkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouwen.html>vrouwen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanzienlijke.html>aanzienlijke</a> levensstanden <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beschaafde.html>beschaafde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kringen.html>kringen</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 6, page 195.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunstenaar.html>kunstenaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> alzoo degeen, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:overeenstemming.html>overeenstemming</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> idée <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> den <a href = vnd.unilang:vorm.html>vorm</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aanschouwelijk.html>aanschouwelijk</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">An artist <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> therefore the person, who brings this correspondence of an idea with the form to fruition in a <b>visible</b> work.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">empirical</span>
<ul><li><b>1947</b>, P. <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Schilfaarde, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zin.html>zin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geschiedenis.html>geschiedenis</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> wijsgerige <a href = vnd.unilang:bespreking.html>bespreking</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> den <a href = vnd.unilang:gang.html>gang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensheid.html>mensheid</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 2, page 248.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">Ten <a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opgemerkt.html>opgemerkt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>zij</a> [cultuurwetenschap] <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aanschouwelijk.html>aanschouwelijk</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:evenals.html>evenals</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:natuurwetenschap.html>natuurwetenschap</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aanschouwelijke.html>aanschouwelijke</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:betrekking.html>betrekking</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Let it be mentioned in the first place, that the [the humanities] are <b>empirical</b>, just like natural science <a href = vnd.unilang:concerns.html>concerns</a> the <b>empirical</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> using images and pictures</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanslaan.html>aanslaan</a> (20635)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenslaen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slaan.html>slaan</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanslaan.html>aanslaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to strike physically so as to activate or produce an effect</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tax (a taxable person) with a tax assessment</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start, to kick in, to switch on</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of a dog</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start barking <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">as a sign of <a href = vnd.unilang:alarm.html>alarm</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to succeed, to have an effect</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to catch on, to become popular

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanslag.html>aanslag</a> (3166)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenslach</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenslaen</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slach</i> (modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanslaan.html>aanslaan</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slag.html>slag</a></i>). Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">on</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slag.html>slag</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">strike, hit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aensprâke</i>. <li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> charge, accusation, legal claim</li></ol>

***aanspreken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanspreken.html>aanspreken</a> (10635)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aensprēken</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spreken.html>spreken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanspreken.html>aanspreken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to address</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to accost</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanstekelijk.html>aanstekelijk</a> (41166)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aansteken.html>aansteken</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanstekelijk.html>aanstekelijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanstekelijk.html>aanstekelijker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">aanstekelijkst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">contagious</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">infectious</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">easily infecting others</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">catchy</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">highly memorable</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
